 iske baad pakistan ke pradhanmantri imran khan ne mangalvaar ko bharat ko bharosa dilaayaa ki agar bharat pulavama aatankwaadi hamale main ‚Äòkarrwai yogya khufia jaankaree'saajha karata he to sajeeshkartaaon ke khilaaf karrwai kii jaaegi

 However, the two unions included in the UFBU, the National Organization of Bank Workers and the National Organization of Bank Officers, are not involved in the strike
 in sanghathanon ne is hadtaal ko raajnneeti se prabhavit kadam bataaya he

 tippaniyan All India Bank Officers Confederation (AIBOC) general secretary Harvinder Singh said, "the strike program is going on as no action was taken by the bank management especially the Indian Banks' Association (IBA) to suspend it
 ' ol india bank emplayes associysan (eibiie) ke mahasachiv sietch venkatchalam ne kaha ki mukhya shram ayukta ne bank prabandhan or karmchaaree sanghathanon ke bich 21 farvari ko ek sahmati baithak karai thi lekin isamen bank prabandhan ke adiyal rakh ke kaaran baithak main koi sakaaratmak parinaam nahin niklaa

 ' The Economic Survey 2016-17 suggested the establishment of a 'bad bank', so that the bad debts of banks (called non-performing assets) can be dealt with
 isamen kaha gaya he ki centre sarkaar ek sampatti purnvas agency kaa gathan karen, jo fanse hue karjo ko bainkon se kharid kar uskaa boj uthaae, taaki bainkon ke karj kaa boj kam karne kaa kathin raajnneetik faisla liya ja sake
